<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery( function( $ ) {
	$( 'body' )
		.addClass( 'is-js' )
		.delegate( '.p2-task-list :checkbox', 'click', function() {
			var $this = $( this ),
			    $li = $this.parents( 'li:first' ),
			    $form = $this.parents( 'form:first' ),
			    data = $li.find( ':input' ).serialize(),
			    colorEl = $li, origColor = $li.css( 'background-color' ), color;

			while ( colorEl.get(0).tagName && colorEl.css( 'background-color' ).match( /^\s*(rgba\s*\(\s*0+\s*,\s*0+\s*,\s*0+\s*,\s*0+\s*\)|transparent)\s*$/ ) ) {
				colorEl = colorEl.parent();
			}

			color = colorEl.get(0).tagName ? colorEl.css( 'background-color' ) : '#ffffff';

			data += '&ajax=1&' + $form.find( '.submit :input' ).serialize();

			$.post( $form.attr( 'action' ), data, function( response ) {
				if ( '1' === response )
					$li.css( 'background-color', '#F6F3D1' ).animate( { backgroundColor: color }, 'slow', function() { $li.css( 'background-color', origColor ); } );
			} );
	} );
} );
</script>

height: 116px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Anyone read Balinese? </div> </div> </div> <!-- close group --> <div class="gallery-group images-1" style="width: 158px; height: 120px;" data-original-width="158" data-original-height="120" > <div class="tiled-gallery-item tiled-gallery-item-small"> <a href="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/best-mountain-biking-trail-in-bali-downhill-cycling-from-mount-batur-to-ubud/090-p1030850/" border="0"> <img data-attachment-id="503" data-orig-file="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/090-P1030850.jpg" data-orig-size="600,450" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;Picasa&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1423896523&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.002&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="090-P1030850" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/090-P1030850.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/090-P1030850.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" src="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/02/090-P1030850.jpg?resize=154%2C116" data-original-width="154" data-original-height="116" title="090-P1030850" alt="" style="width: 154px; height: 116px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Last stop &#8211; A cock fighting stadium </div> </div> </div> <!-- close group --> </div> <!-- close row --> </div>
<p>This has to be one the easiest and most varied downhill mountain bike trail I&#8217;ve ever done.</p>
<p>The trail begins at Mount Batur, Bali, with breakfast looking across at the 2,000 metre mountain I&#8217;d trekked up for sunrise the previous Sunday. Unfortunately it was too misty to properly see the mountain, as I did this trail in February, in the midst of Bali&#8217;s rainy season.</p>
<p>After breakfast the mountain bike trail begun, which would take us downhill virtually the entire way on the 35km back to Ubud. Literally, you hardly have to pedal and just need to use the breaks, so anyone can do this no matter how daunting the distance might sound.</p>
<p>This mountain bike trail takes you through forests, towns rice fields, past temples and you even get invited to look around a Balinese house, or should I say compound. Families stick together in Bali, and children continue to live in the same compound as their parents even when they&#8217;ve grown up, with the whole family sharing their own private Hindu temple.</p>
<p>This is one of the best mountain bike trails in Bali &#8211; it&#8217;s easy on the thighs and the eyes with beautiful countryside and rice paddies surrounding you nearly the entire way. There&#8217;s no shortage of companies that offer this trail, and being Bali you&#8217;re looking at 30 USD or less for the whole day. So an absolute bargain to boot!</p>
	</div>

	
	
	<div class="bottom-of-entry">&nbsp;</div>

height: 238px;" data-original-width="316" data-original-height="238" > <div class="tiled-gallery-item tiled-gallery-item-large"> <a href="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/best-mountain-biking-trails-in-cyprus-one-brutal-hill-and-a-hidden-dam/p1030221/" border="0"> <img data-attachment-id="406" data-orig-file="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/P1030221.jpg" data-orig-size="500,375" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;Picasa&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1413188549&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.004&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="P1030221" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/P1030221.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/P1030221.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" src="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/P1030221.jpg?resize=312%2C234" data-original-width="312" data-original-height="234" title="P1030221" alt="" style="width: 312px; height: 234px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Heading back to Polis </div> </div> </div> <!-- close group --> </div> <!-- close row --> </div>
<p>This summer I was lucky enough to be in Cyprus for my brother&#8217;s wedding combined with my Dad&#8217;s birthday, so decided to take full advantage and check out Cyprus&#8217; best mountain bike trails. After some research, Polis appeared to be the place to go, which is a small town in the north (Greek side) close to Akamas national park. This area of Cyprus is billed as a mountain bikers&#8217; paradise, with loads of trails throughout the park and surrounding countryside.</p>
<p>I rented an Orange Gringo from <a href="http://www.wheeliecyprus.com/" target="_blank">Wheelie Cyprus</a> who kindly delivered it to where I was staying, along with a kit bag with lock, puncture repair kit, map, helmet and gloves. They even offer an emergency pickup service, which is ideal if, like me, you&#8217;re going mountain biking on your own. Thankfully, I didnt need it, but always good to have that reassurance should you have an accident.</p>
<p>Day one I decided to tackle the mountain bike trails around Akamas park. Word of warning &#8211; if you ever go on this trail, whatever you do, make sure you take the trail through Neo Chorio and around the south side. I took a right turning too early and after a pleasant hour or so cycling along the northern coast I had to make a brutal ascent up the mountain. I had to push the bike up a lot of it and took a few breaks, and it took me over an hour to get to the top. At least I could enjoy just sitting and enjoying the scenary on a rapid descent the other side.</p>
<p>Akamas park is packed with wide, open mountain bike trails along dirt tracks and through parkland, and there&#8217;s literally no traffic (cars or people). Just make sure you go round from the south:)</p>
<p>Day two I headed along the coast east to check out a Cyprus mountain bike trail around Argaka park for a circular trail past a dam. There was some uphill climbing to get to the park, but nothing too daunting compared to the previous day. Once you get to park there&#8217;s a mountain bike trail that winds all the way through the valley. I didnt find the dam, but had a great time bombing around the cliffside paths nonetheless.</p>
<p>So if you&#8217;re thinking of doing some cycling on the island, head to Polis in the north for the best mountain bike trails in Cyprus.</p>
	</div>

	
	
	<div class="bottom-of-entry">&nbsp;</div>

height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Looking back towards the north of Prague to where we came from </div> </div> </div> </div> </div>
<p>During the summer I thought I&#8217;d check out Prague in the Czech Republic, central Europe. I was lucky enough to make contact with a local via Meetup.com to show me a mountain biking trail alongside Prague&#8217;s river. The total trip was only about 30km, but featured a variety of terrain, from cycle paths to single lane trails through the woods and steep downhill section on the main road back into Prague.</p>
<p>If you&#8217;re ever in Prague, I recommend renting a mountain bike and exploring the cycle paths around the outskirts of the city. It only takes 5 minutes to escape the city centre and out enjoying the surrounding countryside. There&#8217;s also a couple of Facebook groups for cyclists if you want to find some local cycle buddies to show you the best mountain bike trails around Prague.</p>
	</div>

height: 116px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Back on the main road back to the start </div> </div> </div> <!-- close group --> </div> <!-- close row --> </div>
<p>This mountain bike trek took me through narrow streets of Bangkok, so narrow people literally had to jump out of the way to let us past. But, as always in Thailand, everyone was very accommodating, and I got the impression they&#8217;re used to seeing these mountain bike tours of foreigners coming through their local market. We actually managed to lose our guide at one point so had to stop and wait for him to come back and rescue us.</p>
<p>What&#8217;s more, this mountain bike trail in Bangkok includes a boat trip over to the &#8216;lungs of Bangkok&#8217;. This island offers an escape from the city for the locals, with lots of forests and parkland to explore. So you get a bit of everything on this trip and you really do get to see the authentic side of Bangkok on this mountain bike trek, which takes you through the backstreets and areas you&#8217;d never imagine visiting on your own.</p>
<p>This mountain bike trail in Bangkok was done with <a href="http://www.followmebiketour.com/" target="_blank">Follow Me Bike Tours</a>. The bikes were in great condition, the guide was friendly and helpful and the lunch was absolutely delicious (pedaling 40km is always a great way to build an appetite!). So if you&#8217;re in Bangkok and fancy doing something more adventurous than shopping and visiting temples, I highly recommend going on this mountain bike trail with Follow Me.</p>
<p>When I first saw  this video I thought they couldnt be serious about taking us down these streets!</p>
<p><iframe src="//www.youtube.com/embed/D727tafH6js" width="420" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p>
	</div>

				<a href='http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/mountain-biking-trail-through-the-pine-forests-of-dalat-vietnam/p1020110s/'><img src="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020110s.jpg?resize=150%2C150" class="attachment-thumbnail" alt="Time to head home" aria-describedby="gallery-5-256" data-attachment-id="256" data-orig-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020110s.jpg?resize=500%2C375" data-orig-size="500,375" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1398322190&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.002&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;}" data-image-title="P1020110s" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020110s.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020110s.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" /></a>
			</dt>
				<dd class='wp-caption-text gallery-caption' id='gallery-5-256'>
				Time to head home
				</dd></dl><dl class='gallery-item'>
			<dt class='gallery-icon landscape'>
				<a href='http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/mountain-biking-trail-through-the-pine-forests-of-dalat-vietnam/p1020114s/'><img src="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020114s.jpg?resize=150%2C150" class="attachment-thumbnail" alt="Xuan Huong Lake" aria-describedby="gallery-5-261" data-attachment-id="261" data-orig-file="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020114s.jpg?resize=500%2C375" data-orig-size="500,375" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1398322341&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.00125&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;}" data-image-title="P1020114s" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020114s.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i2.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/P1020114s.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" /></a>
			</dt>
				<dd class='wp-caption-text gallery-caption' id='gallery-5-261'>
				 Xuan Huong Lake
				</dd></dl>
			<br style='clear: both' />
		</div>

<p>After a month in Ho Chi Minh, Vietnam, I headed to De Lat to check out some of the mountain bike trails in Vietnam. This trip was with  Vietchallenge and was their <a href="http://vietchallenge.com/Tours/14/Northern-Challenge" target="_blank">Northern Challenge tour</a>. It covers about 32km through beautiful pine forests and countryside, past the Xuan Huong Lake and then finishing in a local Vietnamese village where they sell handicrafts.</p>
<p>There is a lot of uphill and the roads are still in the process of being built, so the terrain was pretty rocky in parts. But if you enjoy a challenge and like to push yourself, then I highly recommend checking out this mountain bike trail if you&#8217;re ever in Delat, Vietnam. There&#8217;s hardly any traffic and mountain biking through unspolit Vietnamese countryside offers lots of Kodak moments.</p>
<p>If you&#8217;re feeling adventurous, you should also try &#8216;<a href="http://vietchallenge.com/Tour-Category/1/Canyoning" target="_blank">canyoning</a>&#8216;. This is where you abseil down waterfalls and is a &#8216;must do&#8217; for many backpackers and is what draws many of them to Dalat. There&#8217;s also come cliffjumping at the end to keep all adrenaline junkies happy.</p>
	</div>

	
			<div class="discussion" style="display: none">
			<p>
				 <a href='http://mattsmountainbikingadventures.wordpress.com/2014/07/20/mountain-biking-trail-through-the-pine-forests-of-dalat-vietnam/' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Mountain Biking Trail through the Pine Forests of Dalat, Vietnam | mattsmountainbikingadventures</a> is discussing.				<a href="#" class="show-comments">Toggle Comments</a>
			</p>
		</div>

height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Local Cambodian girls trying to sell us postcards </div> </div> </div> <div class="gallery-group" style="width: 210px; height: 210px;" data-original-width="210" data-original-height="210" > <div class="tiled-gallery-item"> <a href="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/temple-mountain-biking-trail-at-angkor-wat-cambodia/p1010742/" border="0"> <img data-attachment-id="207" data-orig-file="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/P1010742.jpg" data-orig-size="500,375" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1394790914&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.004&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;}" data-image-title="P1010742" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/P1010742.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/P1010742.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" src="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/P1010742.jpg?resize=206%2C206" data-original-width="206" data-original-height="206" title="P1010742" alt="" style="width: 206px; height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> </a> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> We didnt buy any, so they sang to us instead </div> </div> </div> </div> </div>
<p>The <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angkor_Wat#Site_and_plan" target="_blank">Angkor Wat</a> temples are a must on any trip to Cambodia. This incredible temple complex, whose name literally translates to &#8216;City of Temples&#8217; dates  to the 12th century. It is the largest religious monument in the world. First built for Hindu then Buddhist worship during the time of the Khmer Empire, the temples span a huge area. So rather than go on foot or in the back of a tuk tuk, I decided to do some mountain biking around the temples.</p>
<p>There are a few companies to choose from, but I opted for the <a href="http://www.kko-cambodia.org/html/OffRoad.php" target="_blank">KKO&#8217;s (Khmar for Khmar Organisation) </a>organised mountain biking trail. The main reason was because the money goes towards supporting 250 local people in gaining valuable skills, like speaking English or learning to become a mechanic, so they can find work and raise the general community out of poverty.</p>
<p>This mountain bike trail took us on a 40 km loop around 5 temples, namely Bayon, Ta Nei, Preah Khan, Prasat Chung and Bantang Kdei. While we didnt go to Angkor Wat itself, I visited this on sunrise on another occasion. We covered a lot of ground, but you really need three days to see the temples properly and fully appreciate the history behind what you&#8217;re seeing.</p>
<p>Our guide was very informative, you get taken to some places most tourists don&#8217;t see and the bikes were in excellent condition, so I highly recommend checking out <a href="http://www.kko-cambodia.org/html/OffRoad.php" target="_blank">KKO&#8217;s website</a> if you&#8217;re looking to do a mountain bike trail around Angkor Wat, Cambodia.</p>
	</div>

				<dd class='wp-caption-text gallery-caption' id='gallery-7-198'>
				The iconic wooden bridge back into Luang Prabang
				</dd></dl>
			<br style='clear: both' />
		</div>

<p>While on a 10 day visit to Luang Prabang in Laos, checking out the local mountain biking trail was a priority. I did a guided tour with <a href="http://www.laos-adventures.com/" target="_blank">Tiger Trail Laos</a> covering 60km from Luang Prabang and around a great loop through the countryside. As you can imagine, the scenery was breathtaking, with hardly any traffic and surrounded by the unspoiled countryside of Laos. People were also very friendly, with children running out from their homes to shout &#8216;Sa Ba Dee!&#8217; (hello) as we cycled past. Lets hope this friendly sentiment continues because Luang Prabang is undergoing some rapid changes now that tourism has arrived.</p>
<p>If you&#8217;re ever in Laos, I highly recommend going on some mountain biking trails while you&#8217;re there. My big regret was not cycling to the popular waterfall because I was worried I&#8217;d get lost without a guide. Turns out it&#8217;s more or less a straight road all the way.</p>
<p>I hope to go to Laos again some day and try out some of the mountain biking trails around the<a href="http://travelhappy.info/laos/the-plain-of-jars-laos/" target="_blank"> Plain of Jars.</a> Maybe next year&#8230;</p>
	</div>

	
			<div class="discussion" style="display: none">

		</div>

				<dd class='wp-caption-text gallery-caption' id='gallery-8-167'>
				Back in Chiang Mai, with Doi Suthep in the background
				</dd></dl>
			<br style='clear: both' />
		</div>

<p>The beauty of mountain biking around Chiang Mai, Thailand, is that it&#8217;s flat as a pancake. What&#8217;s more there&#8217;s a route you can take from the south of the city which takes you along country lanes all the way with barely any traffic. On this trip I went cycling through forests and past rice fields on a scenic mountain bike trail around the temples and remnants of Wiang Kum Kam, the old capital of the Chiang Mai province. As I hope the photos show, it was an exceptionally picturesque mountain bike trail with lots to see and a great way to escape the crowds to do some truly authentic sight seeing.</p>
	</div>

height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Was it left or right? </div> </div> </div> <div class="gallery-group" style="width: 210px; height: 210px;" data-original-width="210" data-original-height="210" > <div class="tiled-gallery-item"> <img data-attachment-id="82" data-orig-file="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000898.jpg" data-orig-size="600,450" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1382518469&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;80&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.01&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;}" data-image-title="1P1000898" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000898.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000898.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" src="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000898.jpg?resize=206%2C206" data-original-width="206" data-original-height="206" title="1P1000898" alt="" style="width: 206px; height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> Fellow riders and our guide in the middle </div> </div> </div> <div class="gallery-group" style="width: 210px; height: 210px;" data-original-width="210" data-original-height="210" > <div class="tiled-gallery-item"> <img data-attachment-id="83" data-orig-file="http://bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000900.jpg" data-orig-size="600,450" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;2.8&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;DMC-FS7&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;1382527342&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;5.5&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;100&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0.033333333333333&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;}" data-image-title="1P1000900" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000900.jpg?fit=300%2C300" data-large-file="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000900.jpg?fit=1024%2C1024" src="http://i1.wp.com/bestmountainbiketrails.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/06/1P1000900.jpg?resize=206%2C206" data-original-width="206" data-original-height="206" title="1P1000900" alt="" style="width: 206px; height: 206px;" data-recalc-dims="1" /> <div class="tiled-gallery-caption"> My first mountain biking induced stiches </div> </div> </div> </div> </div>
<p>This was my first experience of downhill mountain biking and it was certainly a case of baptism by fire, or rather rainwater. After checking in at <a href="http://www.mountainbikingchiangmai.com/" target="_blank">Mountain Biking Chiang Mai</a>, we were taken up to the top of Doi Suthep by taxi, or Song Thau as they&#8217;re called in Thailand. We started in glorious sunshine but it poured it down for the 40mins or so it took to get to the top. After unloading the bikes and doing a quick proficiency test, which involved showing we could cycle over a log, it was time to hit the very skiddy slopes.</p>
<p>I later discovered that under these conditions I should have got a bike with disc brakes. Unfortunately I had the normal rubber brakes, which werent much use on the mud slicks we had to cycle down. With the brakes largely ineffective, it was feet down most of the way on this muddy mountain bike trail, although there were some intermittent dry parts to have some fun on.</p>
<p>My confidence wasnt too high at this stage, being my first time downhill, which I think contributed to the number of times I fell off. I was fully padded up though and can handle a few bumps. It wasnt until I got to the bottom though that I noticed that I had a big gash in my leg just before going through a quick dip in the lake where the ride ends. Thankfully we had a doctor in our group who recommended I get stitched up, leading to my first mountain bike induced scar.</p>
<p>Despite the muddy conditions, I had a great time, and this just fed my enthusiasm for mountain biking and seeing what other trails are out there. with a variety of mountain bike trails to choose from, with the full range of skill levels, I recommend checking this out if you want to do any downhill mountain biking when in Chiang Mai, Thailand.</p>
	</div>

	
	
	<div class="bottom-of-entry">&nbsp;</div>

					var returnValue = addComment._Jetpack_moveForm( commId, parentId, respondId, postId ), cancelClick, cancel;

					if ( false === returnValue ) {
						cancel = document.getElementById( 'cancel-comment-reply-link' );
						cancelClick = cancel.onclick;
						cancel.onclick = function() {
							var cancelReturn = cancelClick.call( this );
							if ( false !== cancelReturn ) {
								return cancelReturn;
							}

								return cancelReturn;
							}

							comm_par = 0;

							tellFrameNewParent();

							return cancelReturn;
						};
					}

					if ( comm_par == parentId ) {
						return returnValue;
					}

					comm_par = parentId;

					tellFrameNewParent();

					return returnValue;
				};
